Just as she exhaled, her once somber demeanour had changed. Her eyes were piercing as she looked toward the boy.

<font color = white>&#34;Oi, oi, oi.. Who tha&#39; heck do ya&#39; take me for? Some kinda&#39; bum? Only one here who&#39;s gonna be makin&#39; sandwiches fer&#39; you is yer&#39; mum. Now buzz off &#39;fore I throw ya&#39; in the water!&#34;</font> she retorted. Her tone was vulgar and riddled with slang. Her once prim-and-proper way of speaking had vanished at the drop of a hat and she&#39;d tilted her nose up, even if she were shorter she found a way to still look down her nose at the boy. She almost seemed like a bit of a delinquent in the moment.</font></font></font>
